20-Apr-26 13:15:23 - Balaji Manikanta Sai Sadhu (Additional comments)
Hello @Carol Osborne,

I have tested the scenario in the test environment, and below are my observations:

Scenario 1: - 
I created and published a Knowledge Base (KB) article, making myself the owner.
I then logged in as you and edited the article, saving it as a draft.
When I checked your “My Draft Articles” queue, the article did not appear there.

Scenario 2: - 
I logged in as you and created a KB article, making you the owner.
I then edited the same article and saved it as a draft.
In this case, the article appeared correctly in your “My Draft Articles” queue.

Conclusion: -
The behavior is working as designed based on the filters configured in the personal view:

Only KB articles created by you and saved as draft by you are displayed in the “My Draft Articles” view.
KB articles not created by you, even if you edit them and save them as drafts, do not appear in this view.

This is due to the criteria defined in the personal view filter.
Please let me know if you have any questions or need further clarification regarding this testing.

Regards,
Balaji.

13-Apr-26 16:31:49 - Balaji Manikanta Sai Sadhu (Additional comments)

Hello Team,

I am moving this request to the L2 team for a fix.

Requirement Overview: - The requestor needs a report that clearly identifies at which approval level a Geo Code change request is currently pending, and which approval team or user is responsible.

When a Geo Code change is submitted for an account, the request follows an approval workflow involving multiple levels, primarily: Sales Operations, Finance.

Currently, there is no reliable visibility into:
Whether the request is pending at Sales Ops or Finance
Which approver (role or user) is the request waiting on
The current approval status at each level

Existing reporting attempts are not retrieving the required approval-level data, making it difficult to track or follow up on pending requests.

https://progress.lightning.force.com/lightning/r/Report/00OPb00000LziG9MAJ/view - This report can give the data of approved stages, but not pending approval.

Please check the screenshot attached below from where the data needs to be pulled.

Regards,
Balaji.

Hello Team,

I am moving this request to the L2 team for a fix.

Requirement Overview: - The requestor needs a report that clearly identifies at which approval level a Geo Code change request is currently pending, and which approval team or user is responsible.

When a Geo Code change is submitted for an account, the request follows an approval workflow involving multiple levels, primarily: Sales Operations, Finance.

Currently, there is no reliable visibility into:
Whether the request is pending at Sales Ops or Finance
Which approver (role or user) is the request waiting on
The current approval status at each level

Existing reporting attempts are not retrieving the required approval-level data, making it difficult to track or follow up on pending requests.

The requestor seeks confirmation on whether an existing security solution is in place to scan and validate file attachments uploaded by customers through the Community Portal or received via Salesforce email. 

Specifically, the objective is to understand:
1) Whether any current security software or platform is actively scanning these attachments for threats (e.g., malware, viruses, or malicious content).

3) If no solution is currently implemented, whether there are plans to introduce or implement an attachment-scanning or email security solution in the future.

This information is required to assess the current security posture and identify any potential gaps or planned enhancements related to attachment security within Salesforce.
